puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then it should be rubbed on its neck between your hands and loosen the thighs; 
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then extend the heart above, and scrape all the skin of the buttocks along the length;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then put inside the lips of the waist one-inch incisions according to what you need to open the wound, and be such that the pus can come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then flay the pus that is under the skin of the buttocks, so that the white pus hard is uncovered on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then put your index finger in what follows the buttock, in what is between the white pus that is under the skin of the thigh, and between the second pus, and detach what is behind the thigh, and between the second pus;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then place the left hand inside the testicles and extend the white cord upwards towards your left hand, and lift the egg towards all the white cord toward the waist; 
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the minister to extend the egg upwards, and loosen what is behind the bandage; 
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and ask at your feet if there is any intestine wrapped around or hard white cord, and if you find none, push it into the belly below; 
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle with a large thread made of ten threads, and insert it into the back part of the cord, which is after the skin of the testicles; 
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after the waist, then cut the heads that appear from the threads, as long as there are four threads;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then assemble them one on top of the other in a cross shape, and tie the cord, which we said is below the skin of the testicles, with a strong tie of two parts; 
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the head of the shoulder with threads, and tie it in two parts, so that none of the vessels that nourish it can enter, lest an abscess arise. 
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	And place a second tie above the first one, twice as long as that, and after these two ties leave two fingers' breadth below the pit of the chest. 
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	And afterward all the rest according to the roundness which an egg carries.  
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	Then cut into the part below the skin of the chest, as much as the sinews allow, and the gut, as we have said before. 
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	Then apply wool moistened with oil to the wounds, and place it upon them, and then apply the tie that we have mentioned. 
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And never cauterize white flesh as we have said, after the incision, for fear of stopping the flow of blood.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens often, and leave the tie until it oozes through.
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it delays in the chair, so be it raised with hot water, and put on what we have said, as long as it discharges; 
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment, until it is perfectly healed. 
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch I never saw anyone who dared to make the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made as the branch which is together with the vine, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after the incision on top lightly underneath; 
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut it in half, and treat the abscess with what works, until the vessels discharge;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.  
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes a rupture comes in the angles, as we have said, and opens the limbs; 
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and none of the intestines are drawn out as coils, and if any are drawn out, it is bad, and repair every hour; 
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	And if it remains too long in this position, the wound or fistula grows, until the intestines protrude. 
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	And this happens by the extension of the fistula which is at an angle, as we have said, for it is stretched, then softened and swollen, and opened. 
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	And the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before. 
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	And sometimes it is cured with iron in this manner: 
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	And that the patient lies often on his back between your hands, then mark the place of the rupture swollen for three fingers wide.  
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	And then extract the fistula which is below the skin that has become accustomed to it, then take a thread and place it on the spot apparent of the fistula. 
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	And press at the depth of the belly, then sew the two apparent places of the fistula onto the head of the thread, and sew one and the other. 
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	Then extract the head of the right [bone], and do not cover the bone nor extend the bone or anything else, as I have shown you in the treatment of the fracture of the intestines; 
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then treat it by the treatment of wounds.  
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, if the patient cleanses and heals the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The syfac is constrained, and has no appearance in the fracture, and the cauteries are muted in this place, and closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	from the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the skin of the testicles is softened in some men, because the vessels within are softened, and it is made to be seen; 
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And it is necessary, when one wishes to treat it, that one make the patient lie on his back, and cut the softened skin onto the natural skin;  
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then bring together the two lips at one suture, and if you see it, first sew the excess of the softened skin to three or four sutures firmly; 
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then cut between the sutures, and treat it like the other wounds, until it is healed, and remove the thread.  
dou chastrement	Through chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castrations are begun in our law, and for this reason it would please me not to speak of them in this book; 
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and they are only necessary for two ways:  
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one is that the mire responds in kind when one asks it and in kind the cure; 
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need to castrate certain beasts to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other beasts. 
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say therefore that castrations are done in two ways: 
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by attraction or by incision.  
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In that which we do by attraction, we make the beast sit in hot water until the testicles are softened and hang down; 
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them with your hand until they are drawn back and you no longer feel them. 
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the castration of the loins: 
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	It is necessary that you hold the beast, and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut on each testicle one cut, when you have well skinned them; 
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	And leave no spot so that the facial skin and the subtle facial skin which is upon the vessels; 
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	And this manner of castration is better than that which is done by traction, for because in traction some part of the testicles may remain by chance, by which the beast desires lust; 
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then heal the wound until it is healed. 
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphroditism is according to two manners like men:  
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	One is when between the two testicles appears also like the shape of a woman's nature, or it has hair, and sometimes passes urine through it.  
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other manner is in women, and has upon the breast as a rod and two horns.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for man and woman is such that you cut away all the attached flesh, and treat it like other wounds. 
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second manner, for men whose urine passes through the skin of their testicles, there is no cure. 
de la tentigene	from the tenting
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	A tentigine is an attached flesh on the natural part, as long as it is too ugly to see;  
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have them as large as a hand, and this is the treatment. 
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is fitting that you hold the excess of the tentigine in your hand or at a knife point and cut it lightly;  
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, so that blood does not flow, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed. 
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	And there is another flesh that grows at the mouth of the bladder, and it bleeds, and sometimes bursts, and it is according to the appearance of a cow, and because of this the ancients called it "cow disease." 
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	It is necessary that you treat it as we have said about the tentigine, and cure it until it is healed.
de erratique	Of a wandering [bone]
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is erratic when the nature of a woman is not perceived, or when the openings are small; 
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural by birth, or accidental by illness that it has come;  
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is by char added, or through subtle artifice or species, and it is made perfect in the marrow, or in the ribs, or below, or wherever it may be;  
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and they defer conception, and childbirth, and perhaps having flowers; 
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of these is by the regard of the belly.  
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the splinters are close together, appearing so at your right or left hand.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is through subtle artifice, and it is close to two pounds, if you hurry, then do this:  
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Put your two index fingers together, and the woman should be on her back, spread her legs; 
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then stretch the two pounds until the subtle artifice is gone, and the inflammations are over; 
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool and moisten it with oil and put it on the place and let the woman rest at home every day so that she cannot lift. 
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the bone is hard and thick, you must cut it with a spatulum resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the swelling is from fresh meat, suspend it to the loin and the hip; 
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the medicines well-seasoned with blood, such as agaric, dragon's blood, frankincense, together with plenty of egg yolk. 
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then apply a cane of plumb large enough so that the wound cannot close; 
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and thus for a long time, and apply a tent of dry linen; 
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then it should be cured with other remedies until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when a sore appears on the sea, if it should be covered according to this manner, unless it is an abscess or ulcer.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an infected abscess which is in the flesh one must not touch it with fire.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins which do not usually accustom themselves to, and when hemorrhoids are old they become swollen. 
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And we have said in the division the resemblances of wounds, and the signs, and I will say here those which receive cure. 
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and fistulas, when they are deeply embedded in the anus, and do not appear to the touch, unless they are cured by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the marsh, one can feel, are those one can cure.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	It is necessary then that you put the woman in a cold house, then extract the tumor with forceps, and cut off the cap on its roots, then sprinkle powders of medicines that restrain blood, such as alum and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things. 
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then plunge her feet into water for an hour, then put her in cold water.  
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if blood flow occurs, let her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate rind and gall and similar things, then take barley flour and mix it with honey and oil, and make a plaster on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it extinguishes, it is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, apply cupping glasses to the back and breasts without injuring.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take wool, and moisten it with plantain juice or with elderberry juice mixed with old wine, and apply it to the place. 
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess subsides, care for the place with ointment until it is healed;  
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called “albathir” is red, and resembles the sharp edge of a knife, if it needs to be covered as I have said for the lultel. 
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then care for it until it is healed. 
des apostemes de la marris	of abscesses of the sea
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses come in the flesh, such as ulcers and gangrenous abscesses and herpes and inflammations and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases which I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is therefore necessary that I say in this treatise about the hot abscess which comes on the marrow, which is not like the abscesses that swell. 
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you want to know the work of iron, look and see if the abscess is hot at the beginning of its appearance, full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red when you can see it. 
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce, but let it rest until the pain is eased; 
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	And then make the patient sit on a stool, and have two small stools where he can lean, and let him rest on his back and bring together his feet at the sides of the leg; 
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	And let his thighs be spread apart, and put his arms below his knees, and tie them well with a good bandage; 
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then suck the side towards the right side, and he will bring the instrument with which one works the mouth of the wound, from which afterwards comes the shape;  
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you see this instrument being administered, you first insert the point to know the depth of the wound, so that what enters within the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and that it does not injure the patient; 
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloths so that the instrument does not injure it. 
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and he must put the horn of the instrument on top and hold the instrument. 
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens and it is made soft with the hand, if necessary, cover it at the head, apply the spatula.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the bowels are emptied, you must put softened tents in the wound, in rose oil or in dry verdigris oil.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and put the tent firmly from the wound to the depth of the wound, and put above the wound and on the handle clean linen soaked in water or vinegar that has been cooked. 
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then cure it after two days with ointment suitable for this purpose until it is healed. 
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and at no time lift it up but moisten the wound with an enema of vinegar and honey, then of vinegar or lily roots and long-cooked aristolochia. 
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to ointment. 
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is filled in the margin, it is necessary that you refrain from cauterizing with iron, but cure it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first for the midwife to know the figure of natural childbirth, and the signs if she sees the woman hasten downwards, and desire to smell the air. 
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child will hasten strongly to be born.  
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	Then you know that this childbirth is according to the natural figure, and the issue is under its head, and the afterbirth with it.  
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	And when you see these signs, it is fitting to press her belly lightly so that the child is born quickly. 
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	For when it descends head first, the afterbirth comes with it and the womb is cleansed of its superfluities by good cleansing.  
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	And this which comes otherwise does not come naturally. 
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it comes sometimes upon its feet, and comes strong against the body or the shoulder, and the hands, where it comes upon its belly, or often, and is converted by chance out of its neck, and by other evil figures; 
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	It is necessary for the midwife that she be wise and subtle in these things, and beware of error and deceit, and I will show you all the figures how one must help her. 
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes upon its head by natural passage, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and her strength is weak, then have her sit upon a stool, where women hold her; 
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and boil oil or fenugreek seed, and then put the midwife between her thighs a small spatula of which here is its form. 
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	And split the second fingernail, and cut it to its nail until the moisture which is inside comes out. 
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	And press the woman's belly so that the child descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to give the woman an enema of fenugreek mucilage with sesame oil. 
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	Then make her grip and sneeze continuously, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour.  
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	If it is now extracted. 
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands come out strong, then it is necessary that you reset them lightly, little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, then place the woman on a stool, and raise her feet up high. 
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	Then overturn the stool onto the ground, and hold the woman so that she does not fall when it is overturned.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And if their hands cannot enter, and the infant dies, then cut the infant's hands with the knife which is previously placed, and remove the child, and reset it equally. 
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the delivery of the child upon its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the infant comes onto its feet, if it bends forward, you must push it upwards; 
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little, until it is straight; 
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take hold of its feet and extend them little by little. 
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	If it jumps up to its thighs, if ordered, then make it sneeze forcefully.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If it jumps further, God willing. 
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it is not as we have said, so turn it little by little until it is according to the natural shape.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it is light.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come further as we have said, take gum arabic, and oil of sesame, and melted resin, and grind all together in a mortar; 
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and put it on the nature of the woman within and heat this ointment, then make her sit in hot water up to under the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when it is softened underneath, make him a collar of myrrh, and put it underneath, and leave it for an hour; 
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then make her sit on a stool, then make her sneeze and pull out her mouth and nose, and press her belly lightly, for the infant jumps now. 
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the issue of the child upon its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the infant comes in this form, if he puts his hands on his chest little by little; 
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then be swaddled up to his neck, and hang his feet down, and be lying on the bed; 
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold his hands little by little, and then put his hands on the belly, and remove the cushions from underneath, until she is fully revealed below; 
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the infant does not jump, take his feet and move them back and forth, then move the belly upwards, then he pushes with his hands;  
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and suckle the child little by little; 
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	And instruct the woman to take care of herself until the infant is weaned. 
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	Of the delivery of a child who comes forth with one hand outstretched
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to engineer a way to return the hand: 
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If one cannot return it, then have the woman stand up and walk;  
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then have her sit on the bed and straighten her legs out. 
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	Then apply the ointment that I have mentioned;  
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then have her sit on a chair and then study how to return the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and suckle the child according to its natural form, and make her sneeze, and instruct her to take care of herself until the infant is fully weaned.  
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	From the issue of the child upon its neck, and it has spread its hands, and its face turned toward the back of its mother
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that the midwife holds her hand, then turns it little by little, and suckles it gently; 
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when they are equal, put on a plaster of honey and oil as we have said, then tell them to move it little by little 
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, make her sit on a seat, and tell her to hold herself steady  
et la fai esternuer.	and make her sneeze 
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in this same manner to all the second
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes out hard in this manner at the second time, cut the second time to your fingernail until the moisture is emptied
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child can suck on its face and on its neck, cut it from there so it is not held back, and let the child die
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the child inside as far as you have put it as it should be, and tell the woman to hold herself steady at all times 
adonques si istra legierement.	then draw lightly  
de l’issue des gemelz	From the issue of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes none are born III or IV; 
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and it happens often. 
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are a strange thing, and do not live, if they are named;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied and are weaned by the wolf who devours them, which is linked to the buttocks;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they also come forth naturally as one under all, as we have said. 
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they come forth grievously, so the cure as we have said, and be the balm subtle, and make quickly and lightly what it does; 
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do thus as it is worth moving to safety.
de plusors enfans	of several children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the womb I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or more up to XV, and they are all formed in the shape of a child by the measurement of the glorious sage, and it befits that the balm know all this, for by chance similar things happen;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	Do according to what is right. 
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman for a dead child in the womb, as I have said in the section, and it does not come out, and you are forced to work with your hands. 
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	It is necessary that you know if the woman is of sound constitution and does not have any other condition or fear of death. 
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary that the woman be placed on her back, with her head inclined downwards and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And the practitioner must hold her firmly in two places, or tie her to the bed so that she is not moved during the removal of the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the womb with moist oil mixed with marshmallow and fenugreek mucilage and flaxseed. Then anoint her belly with these oils and mixtures. 
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then put the end in lukewarm water, then wherever it bites apply ointments that are suitable for this, and be careful if it is inflamed so that it descends on its head; 
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If it puts the ointments in its eyes or neck or mouth or palate or below the beard or on the temple or near the ribs, and if its descent is on foot, put them on the ankle and lower ribs.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And it is necessary that he hold the ointment in his right hand, and put the curvature between his fingers of his left hand, and apply it to all his hand lightly, and put the ointment in none of these places that we have said, until it comes to the empty thing; 
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the ointment: 
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then put it against the other ointment, or the third if you need it, so that the extractions are equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then they are stretched equally by moving from one side to the other, to make it come out, and let the canines be toothed to hold it, as it is in this form: 
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part remains, anoint the base with some of its two oils, and put them in that part, and draw out the other part; 
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if none remains, put this canine or a higher place, and do this until it all comes out. 
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes in front of the other, and he cannot bring it back due to tightness, it is fitting that you wrap it up on a cloth, until it all comes out; 
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then cut into the joint of the sole or with a knife, and thus you must do it to the other hand, and to both feet. 
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it is stuck in the birth canal, or if it has a sharp point assembled, then you must put the pointed spatula between your fingers, press the head and remove the point. 
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Or you turn it to the instrument which is called "almidach", from which its shape comes with the instruments or chapter that are after this one. 
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And do the same if the child has a large head naturally. 
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	And then pull the bones with forceps, and if the head jumps out and is extracted by force, it should be split, as long as the moisture which is in the birth canal goes out. 
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	And if it cannot come out, cut it into pieces as much as you can.  
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is swollen in the belly or below the ribs, then you must pierce it until the moisture runs out. 
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the infant is on its feet, the attraction is light, and straightening at the mouth of the uterus is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is embedded in the belly or breast, it behooves you to extract it wrapped in a cloth on the hand; 
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and make the belly or breast, so long as the moisture that is there runs out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other members are removed and the head remains, put a ball of your hand upon the wound, and pull it to the mouth of the wound; 
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then put one or two pincers on it, and pull hard;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the wound is constricted by a hot boil that has come, it is not right to work on it, but rather administer moist and greasy things; 
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply poultices, and plasters of mild softening and moistening properties.  
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can put it even, administer what we have said for a live infant;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if there is not enough strength, so the treatment goes in parts, and leave nothing of the second intention. 
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if you administer what we have said in abscesses which come to the marrow. 
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding comes, it should be put on tightly restricting, and administer other treatments. 
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose womb one child had been dead, then she conceived another upon that one, and the other also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, a boil came to him on his arm, and it swelled so much that it opened, and he began to have great pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to heal, and I thought for a long time, and could not stitch the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on a plaster of strong attraction, and one bone came out, and after some days another.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marvelled greatly, for this belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	If I thought these were bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I treated the wound, and handled bones with my hands, until the woman was in a better state;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and I kept the woman for a long time like this, and it would be a little bit of bone at that place; 
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have only recorded this chapter so that when the masters find a foreign thing, they know how to help. 
dou ramener la marris a son leu	Bring back the marrow to its place.
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here follows the form of the pressor, with which we weigh the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at two turns as the head of the two liens. 
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, let the horn be more subtle than the restrictor, and made of ebony or boxwood. 
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And let the mouth be of a fist two fingers wide, and the edge of the trees one must, and in length a palm and a half.  
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And between the two limbs there are two adjustments of this same fist, which are firm on one side and the other, half a palm long or a little more. 
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	And these two adjustments are pushed into the mouth of the marrow to open when one turns the two horns.  
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, is made of ebony or boxwood, according to the appearance of tongs.  
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	And it has two horns and two adjustments, as you see, a palm long and two fingers wide. 
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the vulva open to the instrument, make the woman sit up on her bed with her feet hanging down and her legs open, then insert the two instruments joined together into the vulva, and hold the head of the instrument below between her thighs. 
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand on the whole instrument, just as you did with the pliers equally, according to the amount that you see the mouth of the vulva open, so that the woman does what she wants. 
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all assembled and multiplied in their likenesses.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the midwife has them ready, the work is faster and higher for their quantity.  
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not despair of the instrument until you have prepared it, for its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, it is fitting that you instruct the patient to hold back her breath, and then make her sneeze on purpose, and remove your hands from her mouth and nose. 
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she jumps through it, it is good 
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, he takes a pot and makes a hole or cover, and puts in herbs that can open the mouth of the sore, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia lignea, and centaury; 
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or some of them, are cooked in water over the fire
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then he puts a cane or tube into the pot, and the other end into the mouth of the sore, and lets it stay until the vapors go inside the sore
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then he makes her sneeze, as we have said. 
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second sinew leaps quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment and is not soft, he orders the woman to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or marshmallow mucilage, and then puts it into the sore, and squeezes the second finger. 
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, if she takes it and extends it little by little straight so that the marrow does not break at the extraction; 
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but it is necessary to move it slightly to the right and left, and then pull;  
si venra et se desaerdra.	it will come out and become disentangled. 
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the marrow is narrow, we have said the cure is to sneeze and to smoke herbs; 
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not from all that we have said, be careful not to pull in the opposite direction; 
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the marrow, you tie it to the thigh of the woman, then give her an enema of tetrapharmacon ointment. 
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if she will purge and put it back, and it will come out strong; 
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	But nevertheless, when it ferments, a foul odor arises in the stomach and head, and harms the patient. 
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Therefore suitable fumigations are necessary for this: 
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	None of the ancients have tried fumigation of cress and dried figs. 
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one smokes the woman for the retention of flowers and the afterbirth is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it appears similar to a cane, and one puts the subtle head in the fire, and the wide heads on the fire; 
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And let the fumigation be over the coals, until the rash is gone, and begin another. 
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have a pierced fundament, but rather it is closed by a subtle membrane:  
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore the midwife must pierce that membrane with her finger, and not pierce it with a sharp spatula, and guard against touching the wound.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then put it on linen softened in wine and oil, then treat it with ointment until it is healed. 
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will remain set, insert or put a cane of lead in and leave it for three days, and let it be removed when the child wants to go into its chamber.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this swelling comes from the suppuration of a wound or an abscess; 
si covient coper celui soudement:	If it is necessary to cover that suppuration: 
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	if it is cured, as we have said of the chain of lead. 
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come below the buttocks are nodules, and thickenings that come from the buttocks upward, or in the space of two parts, whether there is one fistula or several. 
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when that thickening is old, it works, and still brings forth white or subtle pus, and sometimes these fistulas persist.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are known by the fact that there is either excretion or flatulence when the patient has a bowel movement, and perhaps even one jumps out. 
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if there are fistulas that extend to the bladder, and to the middle of the penis; 
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach the junction of the thigh, and to the base of the buttocks. 
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes a fistula extending to the fundament, and not extending: 
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you place your index finger or thumb on the fundament, and insert a fine needle of silver or iron into the fistula when there is no crookedness. 
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is crookedness, then insert a tent of fine linen, or a horsehair, until you feel the tent or hair with your finger; 
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and nothing comes out through the opening, neither feces nor gas nor worms as we have said: 
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not perforate;
si te haste dou curer.	if you hurry with the cure 
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula extends as far as the bladder or as far as the urinary tract, then the urine escapes and cannot be sealed by medication.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced up to the joint of the thigh, so is the tendon coming up to the place; 
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no crookedness and the invention of pain around it, so it becomes well again, and neither medicine nor ointment is worthwhile; 
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these fistulas there is no stronger cure than work, and vanity of foolish wonders that get involved. 
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the one that is not pierced and is not old, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on his back; 
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and lift their legs up to their thighs, and put their thighs inclined towards their belly;  
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then thrust a tent of iron, or of lead if there is crookedness, as far as you know where the tendon comes. 
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the buttocks, you must stick your index finger in, and then feel if the thread has gone through. 
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And whether it is uncovered or you feel between your finger the sinew or flesh, then know that it has passed through. 
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If it does not work a little, it cannot be healed. 
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	They say that one can heal some well, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And the help that is done is that one heats a subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula as it has been said before. 
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	And they put all of it hot into the fistula until it comes out near the buttocks.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	And do this two or three times as long as you know that those faulty sinews are burned, which resemble a bird's feather.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	And then treat it with tents softened in butter until the flesh dries, then treat it with ointment that hardens and binds. 
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is healed like this, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this cannot be healed otherwise; 
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if the tent enters and does not pierce through to the bone which is at its foundation, and there is between your finger and the tent a thick covering of flesh or of sinew, and you see the fistula under this covering from the heart;  
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the point of the beginning of the fistula appears and protrudes before the tent, and then apply the cautery afterwards until it reaches the head of the tent;  
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the tent will be delivered and will fall out; 
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then cleanse those damaged flesh parts that resemble a bird's feather, and let nothing remain.  
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the blood comes, and cuts between you and the work, then cauterize it with fire or medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery accomplishes two good things: 
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	This is to know, the cautery of these added carts, and the extraction of blood and the drying of moisture. 
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then the treatment of softened tents in butter or crushed cheese, as long as the fire burns hot, and it has burned the carts in the wound.  
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with ointments smeared on hard charcoal, and these are dry medicines. 
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula reaches as far as the base of the body and is distant from the body, it should be plugged at its root or base, and inquire about this.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between II is the cloth or the silk or carts, where it is about to pierce, if there are only signs of faith and hope, by the administration of one of the three methods: 
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	You either cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it out to the bottom, or if you can, put tents and treat it as first. 
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And do not go too far in depth, lest you cut the ligament that holds the foundation, and cause involuntary excretion. 
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then the cure, as we have said; 
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	If it should be healed, then remove the covering and cleanse it after it has been cut near the base, either with a tent or some other pointed instrument. 
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse this rotten flesh that is in the wound as much as you can; 
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then strive to restore the wound and keep the fistula behind the base.
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it is a lighter matter for the patient.  
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And fistulas are never made in this manner: 
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	And when you insert a tent into the fistula and it is near or touching the base of the skin above, then take a tent pierced at its head in this manner:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And I put the twisted thread in two, and put the tent over the whole thread in the fistula until it is at the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it pierces the margin of the base inward, then remove the thread from that piercing so that you insert your finger or thumb. 
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	And treat the head of the thread, and bring the two ends together, and separate one from the other, and leave it for one or two days. 
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And restrain it several times, as long as the threads hold those carriages which are between them, and they intertwine.  
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is healed and clean. 
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open, make it pierce in all the ways you can, if it is not too obstructed.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not right to make a bandage so tight for the placement of the cure, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of a sharp spatula with which one makes a fistula must be very thin on one side and sharp.  
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other side, not so, so that it does not cut what it should not cut, as you see here. 
des emorroydes	Of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Hemorrhoids are according to two manners:  
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	Where they are inside the fundament, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and sometimes bleed, and there is one or several, and they protrude outside the fundament and at the head of the fundament. 
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that are lacking have a bit of moisture, and still now or a bit of sharp citric acid or a bit of blood, and they have the color of the body; 
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment of those who have them in the foundation, if it is so that you instruct the patient to stretch for relief in chambers, until the foundations dry out, and the threads appear; 
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if you hurry, and pinch it with tweezers, or hold it with your fingernail, then cut it at its roots; 
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the lancet cannot hold them because of their moisture, take them with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of chamois; 
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull them out at your leisure, then cut them off and sprinkle some hot powders on top that are in place of a cautery; 
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	where you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter of cautery, then you treat them with other treatments until they are healed. 
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundations cannot come out, give the patient a strong and harsh enema to cleanse what is in the foundation so that it can come out clearly. 
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient complains, and if the threads are strong from the foundation, then the treatment is easy. 
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you take them with your fingernail or with pliers and cut them off, then treat them as we have said until they are healed, and he fears the incision with an iron. 
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	If it is necessary for you to administer a suture in this manner:  
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a twisted thread and put it through a needle, then draw the thread over the top and make the needle pierce through the other side, and turn both ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be wide. 
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and remove the forming thread, then tie the thread, and remove the needle, and do this for all the others, and leave it to correct the excess of blood; 
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then put on the foundation a softened cloth soaked in rose oil or wax, and put it on the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest; 
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave it until they fall out, and when they have fallen, treat them with ointment and other cures until they are healed. 
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	dryness of the veins or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times dryness of humors occurs in the intestine, and by constriction of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you scrape off with the point of a spatula or your fingernail the rind above it so that it does not become moist. 
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it heals as it should; 
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot heal, shave it again more strongly than before until it heals a lot and is scraped. 
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal it until it is healthy. 
dou fremit	Do tremble
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A boil is a small foul appearance on the body, and it goes very deep inside. 
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes one finds coldness there, and one also feels it like a tremor of death, and it comes throughout the body, more in the hands than elsewhere. 
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a cane from a goose feather, or a strong vulture feather, and place that cane on the tremor, until the circles completely encircle the tremor. 
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand on all sides of the cane until you grasp it all around the tremor, and press it deep inside, and pull out the tremor from its roots. 
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see it, make one like this from a chain of iron or steel, and let it be thin underneath and wide on top.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not pierce, but hold tightly to the pain, and press. 
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see it, cauterize the boil as it is shown in the chapter on cautery.  
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes one makes an enema of silver or artichoke, or melted bran or millet; 
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And sometimes one uses small and large instruments, according to those to whom they are administered. 
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore those who are treated in the care of children and who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the enema, both small and large, is wide above, where the belly is tied according to this manner.
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and if there is a blockage where the stomach is bound, as you see, and the excrement remains inside pierced;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and there are two openings on one side and one on the other. 
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and the belly where medicines are placed is made from a bladder of an animal or parchment and pierced all around with small holes, and there is one finger space between each hole, then thread a thick strong twisted raw silk thread through these holes in an X shape or around it, and gather up the belly as if it were a goat. 
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument in front of a strong thread, then administer the enema.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is its circular shape: 
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine be neither too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the clyster with oil or egg yolk, or something similar, then insert it gently; 
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then the minister squeezes it with both hands together until all is expelled, then he withdraws the clyster, and lifts the patient's legs to the wall, and if the medicine wants to come out, let him strain as much as he can; 
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps all night, it is of greater help. 
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you apply a clysma for a disease of loosening of the belly, and the medicine hastens to go, then begin again until it is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are in the fundament or abscess, then let the clyster be as subtle as for a child; 
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the shape of a subtle clyster on which the skin is extracted:  
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have said in the division about the treatment of wounds; 
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Or we will tell you the cures of hands and medicine according to its accomplishment. 
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made with, and according to the places or the wounds where they are made, and by what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by the striking of stone and the cutting of sword and knife or of lance or of musket or of arrow or of similar things. 
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	Or they are made according to the parts of the body, such as a wound that strikes on the neck or on the head or the foot or the belly or the liver and similar members. 
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment of each wound and begin with simple wounds of the head, for remembrance will come in its chapter.
